## **2025 CARE MAPD Prior Authorization Criteria** 

## **Abraxane** 

## **Products Affected** 

- _paclitaxel protein-bound part_ 

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Exclusion**<br>**Criteria**||
|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**|Individual has the applicable mutations based on use/diagnosis.|
|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|1 Year.|
|**Other Criteria**|For melanoma, individual is using as a single agent, second<br>line/subsequent tx and Eastern Cooperative Oncology Group<br>(ECOG) performance status of 0-2. For NSCLC, individual has<br>current ECOG performance status of 0-2.|
|**Indications**|All Medically-accepted Indications.|
|**Off Label Uses**||
|**Part B**<br>**Prerequisite**|No|

## **Adempas** 

## **Products Affected** 

- ADEMPAS 

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Exclusion**<br>**Criteria**||
|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**|For Pulmonary Arterial Hypertension, individual has a right heart<br>catheterization showing all of the following: (a) Mean pulmonary<br>artery pressure (mPAP) greater than or equal to 25 mm Hg at rest<br>(b) Pulmonary capillary wedge pressure (PCWP), mean pulmonary<br>artery wedge pressure (PAWP), left atrial pressure, or left<br>ventricular end-diastolic pressure (LVEDP) less than or equal to 15<br>mm Hg (c) Pulmonary vascular resistance (PVR) greater than 3<br>Wood units. AND Individual has WHO functional class II- IV<br>symptoms. For CTEPH a right-heart catheterization showing a<br>mPAP greater than 25 mm Hg caused by thromboemboli in the<br>pulmonary arterial system (ACCF/AHA 2009).|
|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|1 Year.|



Y0114_25_3012943_0000_I_C                          EFFECTIVE DATE 09/01/2025 1074448MUMENMUB 

4 

--- end of page.page_number=4 ---

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Other Criteria**|For Initial use, for diagnosis of pulmonary arterial hypertension<br>(PAH), WHO Group 1 AND has WHO functional class II-IV<br>symptoms. For diagnosis of chronic thromboembolic pulmonary<br>hypertension (CTEPH), WHO Group 4 AND has WHO functional<br>class II-IV symptoms AND using for one of the following: Persistent<br>or recurrent pulmonary hypertension after at least 180 days<br>following surgical treatment with pulmonary endarterectomey OR<br>Inoperable (via pulmonary endarterectomey) CTEPH. For<br>continued use, there is clinically significant improvement or<br>stabilization in clinical signs and symptoms of disease (including<br>but not limited to improvement in walk distance, dyspnea and/or<br>functional class).|
|**Indications**|All Medically-accepted Indications.|
|**Off Label Uses**||
|**Part B**<br>**Prerequisite**|No|



Y0114_25_3012943_0000_I_C                          EFFECTIVE DATE 09/01/2025 1074448MUMENMUB 

5 

--- end of page.page_number=5 ---

## **AED Agents** 

## **Products Affected** 

- DILANTIN INFATABS 

- DILANTIN ORAL CAPSULE 

- EPRONTIA 

- FYCOMPA ORAL SUSPENSION 

- FYCOMPA ORAL TABLET 

- SPRITAM ORAL TABLET DISINTEGRATING SOLUBLE 1000 MG, 250 MG, 500 MG, 750 MG 

      - TABLET THERAPY PACK 100 & 150 MG 

   - XCOPRI (350 MG DAILY DOSE) 

   - XCOPRI ORAL TABLET 100 MG, 150 MG, 200 MG, 25 MG, 50 MG 

   - XCOPRI ORAL TABLET THERAPY PACK 

   - ZONISADE 

- XCOPRI (250 MG DAILY DOSE) ORAL 

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Exclusion**<br>**Criteria**||
|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**|Diagnosis|
|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|1 Year.|
|**Other Criteria**|Individual has had a trial of and inadequate response or intolerance<br>to ONE of the following preferred agents: Carbamazepine,<br>Clonazepam/ODT, Clorazepate, Diazepam, Divalproex,<br>Ethosuximide, Felbamate, Gabapentin, Lacosamide, Lamotrigine<br>IR, Levetiracetam IR, Oxcarbazepine, Phenytoin, Primidone,<br>Tiagabine, Topiramate IR, Valproate sodium, Valproic acid,<br>Zonisamide OR the preferred agent is not FDA-approved for the<br>prescribed indication.|
|**Indications**|All Medically-accepted Indications.|
|**Off Label Uses**||



Y0114_25_3012943_0000_I_C                          EFFECTIVE DATE 09/01/2025 1074448MUMENMUB

## **Aimovig** 

## **Products Affected** 

- AIMOVIG SUBCUTANEOUS SOLUTION AUTO-INJECTOR 140 MG/ML, 70 MG/ML 

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Exclusion**<br>**Criteria**||
|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**|Episodic migraine defined as at least 4 and fewer than 15 migraine<br>days per month and fewer than 15 headache days per month on<br>average during the previous 3-month period. Chronic migraine<br>defined as a headache occurring on 15 or more days per month for<br>more than 3 months, which, on at least 8 days per month, has<br>features of a migraine headache (ICHD-3 beta).|
|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|Initial: 3 months.  Continuation: 1 year|



Y0114_25_3012943_0000_I_C                          EFFECTIVE DATE 09/01/2025 1074448MUMENMUB 

9 

--- end of page.page_number=9 ---

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Other Criteria**|For initial requests: (I) Individual has a diagnosis of one of the<br>following: (a) Episodic migraine OR (b) Chronic migraine AND (II)<br>Individual is using for migraine prophylaxis. And (III) If individual is<br>also currently using botulinum toxin for prophylaxis and is going to<br>be using Aimovig and botulinum toxin together (i.e., not switching<br>from one agent to another), the following will apply: (a) Individual<br>has had a reduction in the overall number of migraine days or<br>reduction in number of severe migraine days per month with the<br>initial agent AND (b) Individual continues to experience a significant<br>number of migraine headache days or severe migraine days per<br>month requiring additional therapy for migraine prevention. For<br>Renewal requests: (I) Individual has a reduction in the overall<br>number of migraine days or reduction of severe migraine days per<br>month AND (II) Individual has obtained clinical benefit deemed<br>significant by individual or prescriber including any of the following<br>(AHS 2019): (a) 50% reduction in frequency of days with headache<br>or migraine OR (b) Significant decrease in attack duration OR (c)<br>Significant decrease in attack severity OR (d) Improved response<br>to acute treatment OR (e) Reduction in migraine-related disability<br>and improvements in functioning in important areas of life OR (f)<br>Improvements in health related quality of life and reduction in<br>psychological stress due to migraine. AND If individual is using<br>concurrently with botulinum toxin for migraine prophylaxis, the<br>following will apply: Individual has had further reduction in the<br>overall number of migraine days or reduction in number of severe<br>migraine days per month compared to monotherapy with the initial<br>agent (either botulinum toxin or CGRP).|
|**Indications**|All Medically-accepted Indications.|
|**Off Label Uses**||
|**Part B**<br>**Prerequisite**|No|



Y0114_25_3012943_0000_I_C                          EFFECTIVE DATE 09/01/2025 1074448MUMENMUB 

10 

--- end of page.page_number=10 ---

## **Alpha1-Proteinase Inhibitor** 

## **Products Affected** 

## • PROLASTIN-C INTRAVENOUS SOLUTION 

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Exclusion**<br>**Criteria**||
|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**|For Initial use, verified alpha-1 antitrypsin level is less than or equal<br>to 11micro-mol/L (approximately equivalent to 80mg/dL measured<br>by radial immunodiffusion or 57 mg/dL measured by nephelometry)<br>(ATS/ERS 2003, Stoller 2017). Individual has clinically evident<br>emphysema (or chronic obstructive pulmonary disease [COPD]).|
|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|1 Year.|
|**Other Criteria**|For Continued use, there is clinically significant improvement or<br>stabilization in clinical signs and symptoms of disease (including<br>but not limited to decreased frequency of exacerbations, slowed<br>rate of FEV1 decline, preservation of CT scan lung density or<br>improvement in symptom burden).|
|**Indications**|All Medically-accepted Indications.|
|**Off Label Uses**||
|**Part B**<br>**Prerequisite**|No|



Y0114_25_3012943_0000_I_C                          EFFECTIVE DATE 09/01/2025 1074448MUMENMUB

## **Arcalyst** 

## **Products Affected** 

- ARCALYST 

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Exclusion**<br>**Criteria**||
|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**|Written or verbal attestation is provided for confirmation of<br>mutations where applicable based on use/diagnosis. For initial use,<br>for DIRA, disease is in remission from previous anakinra treatment.<br>For Recurrent Pericarditis (RP), individual is using for treatment of<br>RP or reduction in risk of recurrence AND has a history of at least<br>two pericarditis episodes (i.e. presents with at least the third<br>episode) (Klein 2021).|
|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|1 Year.|
|**Other Criteria**|For continued use, individual has been receiving and is maintained<br>on a stable dose of Arcalyst AND mbr has clinically significant<br>improvement or stabilization in clinical signs and symptoms of<br>disease.|
|**Indications**|All Medically-accepted Indications.|
|**Off Label Uses**||
|**Part B**<br>**Prerequisite**|No|

## **Austedo** 

## **Products Affected** 

- AUSTEDO 

- AUSTEDO XR ORAL TABLET EXTENDED RELEASE 24 HOUR 12 MG, 18 MG, 24 MG, 30 MG, 36 MG, 42 

   - MG, 48 MG, 6 MG 

- AUSTEDO XR PATIENT TITRATION 

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Exclusion**<br>**Criteria**||
|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**||
|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**|Individual is 18 years of age or older.|
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|1 Year.|
|**Other Criteria**|For initial requests, Individual has a diagnosis of chorea associated<br>with Huntington?s disease. Has a diagnosis of Tardive dyskinesia<br>confirmed (written or verbal attestation) by the following DSM-5<br>AND (a.) At least 30 days of stable (drug, dose) medication<br>exposure (either typical or first generation antipsychotic agents<br>[such as, chlorpromazine, haloperidol, fluphenazine], atypical or<br>second-generation antipsychotic agents [such as, clozapine,<br>risperidone, olanzapine, quetiapine, aripiprazole], or certain<br>dopamine receptor-blocking drugs used in treatment of nausea and<br>gastroparesis [such as, prochlorperazine, promethazine,<br>metoclopramide]) and (b.) Presence of involuntary athetoid or<br>choreiform movements. For continuation requests, Individual has<br>experienced an improvement in symptoms deemed to be clinically<br>significant by the provider (written or verbal attestation) based on<br>stabilization or improvement in Abnormal Involuntary Movement<br>Scale (AIMS) score (for TD) or total maximal chorea score (for<br>Huntington?s disease).|

## **Baraclude** 

## **Products Affected**

|**Other Criteria**|For initial use: moderate to severe Ankylosing Spondylitis (AS),<br>individual had an inadequate response to/intolerant of ONE<br>conventional therapy [such as, NSAIDs or nonbiologic DMARDS<br>such as sulfasalazine OR has a contraindication to NSAIDs or<br>sulfasalazine. For<br>moderate to severe Psoriatic Arthritis (PsA), individual has had an<br>inadequate response to/intolerant of ONE conventional therapy<br>[nonbiologic DMARDs] (ACR 2019) OR has a contraindication to<br>DMARDs. For Non-radiographic Axial Spondyloarthritis (nr-axSpA),<br>individual has had an inadequate response to, is intolerant of, ONE<br>conventional therapy [such as NSAIDs or nonbiologic DMARDs]<br>(ACR 2019) OR has a contraindication to NSAIDs or DMARDs. For<br>Enthesitis-Related Arthritis (ERA), individual has moderate to<br>severe ERA AND has had an inadequate response to, or is<br>intolerant of, ONE conventional therapy [such as NSAIDs or<br>nonbiologic DMARDs] OR has a contraindication to NSAIDs or<br>sulfasalazine or methotrexate. For HS, individual has had an<br>inadequate response to or is intolerant of conventional therapy<br>(such as oral antibiotics) OR has a contraindication to oral<br>antibiotics. For Continuation use, there is clinically significant<br>improvement or stabilization in clinical signs and symptoms of<br>disease AND has been receiving and is maintained on a stable<br>dose of Cosentyx.|
|**Indications**|All Medically-accepted Indications.|

|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**|Individual is 18 years of age or older, except for the diagnosis of<br>JIA and plaque psoriasis. For PsA and JIA, individual is 2 years of<br>age or older. For plaque psoriasis, 4 years of age or older.|
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|1 Year.|

   - SOLUTION CARTRIDGE 

   - • OMNITROPE SUBCUTANEOUS SOLUTION RECONSTITUTED

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Exclusion**<br>**Criteria**||
|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**|Initial Requests, For idiopathic GHD, has signs/sym of GHD, GV 2<br>SD below age-appropriate mean or ht 2.25 SD below age-<br>appropriate mean and A subnormal (SubNL) response (less<br>than10ng/ml)to 2GH stim tests OR Neonates with hypoglycemia<br>and clinical/hormone evidence of hypopit and low GH (less than<br>10ng/ml)OR 2other pit hormone deficiencies and low IGF-1 OR mbr<br>has cranial irradiation with low IGF1 and normal thyroid tests. Child<br>born SGA(birth wt or length 2 or more SD below the mean for gest<br>age),Child fails to manifest catch up growth by age 4yr(ht 2 or more<br>SD below the mean for age,gender)AND Other causes for SS have<br>been ruled out. Transitioning adolescent: completed linear<br>growth(growth rate of less than 2cm/yr) AND either of the following:<br>A)GH tx has been stopped at least a month and GHD reconfirmed<br>by: 1)idiopathic isolated GHD(SubNL response to 2 GH stim tests<br>OR SubNL response (GH conc of less than10 ng/mL)to 1<br>provocative test and low IGF-I/IGFBP-3) OR 2) multiple pit<br>hormone deficiency,(SubNL response to 1 provocative GH test<br>and/or low IGF-I/IGFBP-3 or 3) with cranial irradiation, low IGF with<br>normal thyroid OR B) any of the following:known genetic mutation<br>assoc with def GH production/secretion or Hypothalamic-pit<br>tumor/structural defect or 3 other pit hormone deficiencies. Adult<br>GHD, mbr has GHD in childhd or docmtd hypopit, hypothal dz,<br>surgery, radiation therapy, trauma, or aneurysmal subarachnoid<br>hemorrhage. GHD confirmed/reconfirmed:SubNL response in<br>adults to 2 GH stim tests (GH conc of less than or equal to 5ng/ml<br>when using insulin induced hypoglycemia OR GH conc of less than<br>or equal to 4.1ng/ml when using arginine)OR SubNL response to 1<br>stim test for adults with hypothalamic or pit dz and 1 pit hormone<br>deficits OR 3 other pit hormone deficiencies.|

For plaque psoriasis, mbr<br>has had an inadequate response to, or is intolerant of,<br>phototherapy or ONE other systemic therapy (e.g. methotrexate,<br>acitretin, or cyclosporine) OR has a CI to phototherapy, acitretin,<br>cyclosporine, and MTX. For uveitis, mbr has<br>chronic, recurrent, treatment-refractory or vision-threatening<br>disease and has had an inadequate response to, or is intolerant of,<br>ONE conventional therapy (such as corticosteroids or<br>immunosuppressants [azathioprine, cyclosporine, or MTX]) OR has<br>a CI to corticosteroids, azathioprine, cyclosporine, and MTX. For<br>chronic, progressive, treatment-refractory Sarcoidosis (Sweiss<br>2014), mbr has had an inadequate response to, or is intolerant of<br>ONE nonbiologic DMARDs (such as methotrexate or azathioprine)<br>OR has a CI to MTX and azathioprine. For dose dense therapy (treatment given more<br>frequently, such as every two weeks instead of every three weeks)<br>for adjuvant treatment of breast cancer. For acute myeloid<br>leukemia and using shortly after completion of induction or repeat<br>induction chemo of AML. For myelodysplastic syndromes (MDS)<br>with severe neutropenia (absolute neutrophil count (ANC) less than<br>or equal to 500mm3 or experiencing recurrent/resistant infection.<br>For mobilization of hematopoietic progenitor cells into peripheral<br>blood for collection by leukapheresis and autologous<br>transplantation. For acceleration of myeloid reconstitution after<br>autologous or allogenic bone marrow transplantation or peripheral<br>blood progenitor cell transplantation. For delayed neutrophil<br>recovery/graft failure after autologous or allogenic bone marrow<br>transplantation. Used to increase survival in individual exposed to<br>myelosuppressive doses of radiation such as Hematopoietic<br>Syndrome of Acute Radiation Syndrome. For malignant melanoma<br>as an adjuvant treatment following surgery for stage III or IV<br>melanoma in those at high risk for recurrence. For<br>relapsed/refractory high-risk neuroblastoma AND using in<br>combination with Danyelza (naxitamab- gqgk) OR is using in<br>combination with dinutuximab (Unituxin), 13-cis-retinoic acid (i.e.<br>isotretinoin) and with or without interleukin-2 (IL-2) (i.e. aldesleukin)<br>AND achieved a partial response to first-line multi-agent, multi-<br>modality therapy (i.e. induction combination chemotherapy, or<br>myeloablative consolidation chemotherapy followed by autologous<br>stem cell transplant).|
|**Indications**|All Medically-accepted Indications.|
|**Off Label Uses**||

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|1 Year.|
|**Other Criteria**|For obstructive sleep apnea/hypopnea syndrome objectively<br>verified by polysomnography (PSG) or home testing with portable<br>monitor showing one of the following (AASM 2017, ICDSD-3): 1.<br>Greater than 15 obstructive events (defined as apneas, hypopneas<br>plus respiratory event related arousal) per hour of sleep OR 2.<br>Greater than 5 obstructive events per hour of sleep and individual<br>reports any of the following: a. Unintentional sleep episodes during<br>wakefulness or b. Daytime sleepiness or c. Unrefreshing sleep or d.<br>Fatigue or e. Insomnia or f. Waking up breath holding, gasping or<br>choking or g. Bed partner describing loud snoring, breathing<br>interruptions or both or h. Presence of comorbid conditions<br>including hypertension, mood disorder, cognitive dysfunction,<br>coronary artery disease, stroke, congestive heart failure, atrial<br>fibrillation or type 2 diabetes mellitus AND 3. Has an Epworth<br>Sleepiness Scale score greater than or equal to 10. For Shift-Work<br>Sleep Disorder (SWSD) defined by all of the following: 1. No other<br>medical disorder or mental disorder accounts for the symptoms<br>AND 2. Symptoms do not meet criteria for any other sleep disorder<br>(i.e. jet lag) AND 3. Symptoms have occurred for at least 3 months,<br>AND 4. Individual has one of the following: a. Individual has<br>excessive sleepiness or insomnia associated with a work period<br>that occurs during the usual sleep phase OR b. Polysomnography<br>demonstrates loss of a normal sleep-wake pattern (such as,<br>disturbed chronobiological rhythmicity). For idiopathic hypersomnia<br>(IH) defined by the following (ICSD-3, Kahn 2015, AASM 2021): 1.<br>Daily periods of irresistible need to sleep or daytime lapses into<br>sleep for more than 3 months AND 2. Absence of cataplexy AND<br>Insufficient sleep syndrome ruled out (if deemed necessary, by lack<br>of improvement of sleepiness after an adequate trial of increased<br>nocturnal time in bed, preferably verified by at least 1 week of wrist<br>actigraphy) AND 3. Multiple Sleep Latency Test (MSLT) shows the<br>following: a. Fewer than 2 sleep-onset rapid eye movement periods<br>(SOREMPs) OR b. No SOREMPs if the REM sleep latency period<br>on the preceding overnight polysomnogram is 15 minutes or less|



Y0114_25_3012943_0000_I_C                          EFFECTIVE DATE 09/01/2025 1074448MUMENMUB 

193 

--- end of page.page_number=193 ---

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
||AND 5. The presence of at least one of the following: a. MSLT<br>showing a mean sleep latency of 8 minutes or less OR b. Total 24-<br>hour sleep time of 660 minutes or longer (typically 12-14 hours) on<br>24-hour polysomnography monitoring (performed after the<br>correction of chronic sleep deprivation) or by wrist actigraphy in<br>association with a sleep log (averaged over at least 7 days with<br>unrestricted sleep) AND 6. Hypersomnolence or MSLT findings are<br>not better explained by another sleep disorder, medical or<br>neurologic disorder, mental disorder, medication use, or substance<br>abuse.|

For EGPA<br>Continuation, tx has resulted in clinically significant improvement or<br>stabilization in clinical signs and symptoms of disease. For HES,<br>mbr has been dx for at least 6 mon AND had trial/inadeq response<br>to oral CS AND mbr experienced 2 or more HES flares w/in the<br>past 12 mon requiring escalation in therapy (increase in oral CS<br>dose or increase/addition of immunosuppressive or cytotoxic<br>therapy) AND has blood eosinophil count greater than or equal to<br>1000 cells/mm3. For HES continuation, tx resulted in clinically<br>significant improvement or stabilization in clinical signs/sx of<br>disease (including but not limited to decrease or absence of HES<br>flares, improvement in fatigue). For CRSwNP, there is presence of<br>nasal polyps demonstrated on either a) anterior rhinoscopy OR b)<br>nasal endoscopy OR c) computed tomography AND mbr had<br>trial/inadeq response to MAINT intranasal CS AND is refractory to<br>or is ineligible or intolerant to systemic corticosteroids OR sinonasal<br>surgery AND mbr is requesting Nucala as add-on therapy to MAINT<br>intranasal CS. For CRSwNP continuation therapy, tx resulted in<br>clinically significant improvement in clinical signs and sx of disease<br>(including but not limited to improvement in nasal congestion or<br>reduced nasal polyp size) AND continues to use Nucala in combo|

|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**|For initial requests, Individual has diagnosis of Pulmonary Arterial<br>Hypertension World Health Organization (WHO) Group 1.<br>Individual has a right heart catheterization showing all of the<br>following: (a) Mean pulmonary artery pressure (mPAP) greater than<br>or equal to 25 mm Hg at rest (b) Pulmonary capillary wedge<br>pressure (PCWP), mean pulmonary artery wedge pressure<br>(PAWP), left atrial pressure, or left ventricular end-diastolic<br>pressure (LVEDP) less than or equal to 15 mm Hg (c) Pulmonary<br>vascular resistance (PVR) greater than 3 Wood units. AND<br>Individual has WHO functional class II- IV symptoms.|
|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|1 Year.|
|**Other Criteria**|Individual is using for the treatment of chronic thromboembolic<br>pulmonary hypertension (CTEPH) OR Individual is using for the<br>treatment of Fontan-Palliated patients. For continuation therapy,<br>there is clinically significant improvement or stabilization in clinical<br>signs and symptoms of disease (including but not limited to<br>improvement in walk distance, dyspnea and/or functional class).|
|**Indications**|All Medically-accepted Indications.|
|**Off Label Uses**||

For<br>Hidradenitis Suppurativa (Hurley stage II or Hurley stage III<br>disease) AND has had an inadequate response to, or is intolerant<br>of, ONE conventional therapy (such as oral antibiotics) OR has a CI<br>to oral antibiotics. |**Other Criteria**|For initial use of replacement therapy, Individual has a dx of (1)<br>primary hypogonadism (congenital or acquired) such as but not<br>limited to: Cryptorchidism OR Bilateral torsion OR Vanishing testis<br>syndrome OR orchitis OR Orchiectomy OR Klinefelter Syndrome<br>OR Chemotherapy OR Toxic damage from alcohol or heavy metals<br>OR idiopathic primary hypogonadism. For Continuation of Testosterone Inj agents for<br>replacement therapy, (a) Individual met all diagnostic criteria for<br>initial therapy and (b) Individual has had serum testosterone level<br>measured in the previous 180 days and (c) Individual has obtained<br>clinical benefits as noted by symptom improvement. - MG/2ML, 75 MG/0.5ML XOLAIR SUBCUTANEOUS SOLUTION 

- • XOLAIR SUBCUTANEOUS SOLUTION RECONSTITUTED 

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Exclusion**<br>**Criteria**||
|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**|Individual has Moderate to Severe Persistent Asthma AND has a<br>positive skin test or in vitro reactivity to a perennial aeroallergen,<br>AND individual has a pretreatment FEV1 less than 80% predicted<br>AND IgE level is equal to or greater than 30 IU/ml. For IgE<br>mediated food allergy, diagnosis is confirmed via clinical hx of IgE<br>mediated food allergy demonstrated by moderate to severe<br>symptoms (including but not limited to throat tightness,<br>dyspnea/wheezing, clinically signification hypotension, generalized<br>urticaria) or requiring administration of epinephrine or emergency<br>medical care AND positive skin prick test or positive serum IgE test<br>or positive food challenge AND has a serum Immunoglobulin E<br>(IgE) level equal to or greater than 30 IU/mL.|
|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|Initial: 6 months. Continuation: 1 Year.|

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Other Criteria**|Initial Treatment: For moderate to severe persistent asthma,<br>individual has had a minimum of 3 month trial and inadequate<br>response or intolerance to ONE combination controller therapy<br>(high dose of inhaled corticosteroids plus long-acting beta-2<br>agonists, Leukotriene modifiers, theophylline or oral<br>corticosteroids)(GINA 2023). Continued treatment beyond 12<br>months is allowed when treatment has resulted in clinical<br>improvement by one or more of the following: Decreased utilization<br>of reliever medications OR Decreased frequency of exacerbations<br>(defined as worsening of asthma that requires increase in inhaled<br>corticosteroid dose or treatment with systemic corticosteroids) OR<br>Increase in percent predicted FEV1 from pretreatment baseline OR<br>Reduction in reported asthma- related symptoms, such as, but not<br>limited to, wheezing, shortness of breath, coughing, fatigue, sleep<br>disturbance, or asthmatic symptoms upon awakening. AND<br>continues to use omalizumab in combination with inhaled<br>corticosteroid-based controller therapy For chronic spontaneous<br>urticaria, individual has had trial and inadequate response or<br>intolerance to ONE potent antihistamine (AAAAI/ACAAI 2014). For<br>continued use for CSU, treatment has resulted in clinically<br>significant improvement or stabilization in clinical signs and<br>symptoms of disease (including but not limited to itch severity and<br>hive count). For initial request for CRSwNP, the presence of nasal<br>polyps have been demonstrated on one of the following (AAO-<br>HNS2015): a) anterior rhinoscopy b) nasal endoscopy OR c)<br>computed tomography AND individual has had trial and inadequate<br>response to maintenance intranasal corticosteroids AND individual<br>is refractory to or is ineligible or intolerant to the following<br>(AAAAI/ACAAI 2014): a) systemic corticosteroids OR b) sinonasal<br>surgery. For CRSwNP continuation requests, tx with Xolair has<br>resulted clinically significant improvement in clinical signs and<br>symptoms of disease (including but not limited to improvement in<br>nasal congestion or reduced polyp size) AND continues to use<br>Xolair in combo with maintenance intranasal corticosteroids. For|
||initial and continued use for IgE mediated food allergy, individual<br>will use omalizumab in combination with food allergen avoidance<br>AND has a prescription for an auto-injectable epinephrine agent.|

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Other Criteria**|For initial tx, of Narcolepsy type 2 (narcolepsy without cataplexy)<br>defined by the following: (1) Daily periods of irrepressible need to<br>sleep or daytime lapses into sleep occurring for at least 3 months<br>AND (2) MSLT with one of the following: (a) MSLT of less than 8<br>minutes and evidence of two SOREMPs (ICSD-3, 2014) or (b) At<br>least one SOREMP on MSLT and a SOREMP (less than 15<br>minutes) on the preceding overnight PSG AND (3) absence of<br>cataplexy AND (4) Exclusion of alternative causes of excessive<br>daytime sleepiness by history, physical exam and PSG. AND (5)<br>Mbr has had a previous trial of and inadequate response or<br>intolerance to TWO of the following medications: (A) One of the<br>following wakefulness promoting medications: (i) Modafinil or (ii)<br>Nuvigil (armodafinil) AND (B) One of the following stimulants: (i)<br>Methylphenidate (ii) Dextroamphetamine or (iii)<br>Amphetamine/dextroamphetamine salt immediate-release OR (6)<br>Trials of wakefulness promoting agents and stimulant agents are<br>not acceptable due to concomitant clinical situations including but<br>not limited to the following: (1) Cardiovascular disease or (2) Drug<br>interactions. Mbr has idiopathic hypersomnia defined by (1) daily<br>periods of strong need to sleep or daytime lapses into sleep for<br>more than 3 mon. (2) absence of cataplexy (3) Insuff sleep<br>syndrome ruled out (if nec, by lack of improvement of sleepiness<br>after adequate trial of increased nocturnal time in bed, preferably<br>verified by at least 1 wk. of wrist actigraphy) (4) MSLT shows fewer<br>than 2 SOREMPs OR No SOREMPs if the REM sleep latency<br>period on the preceding overnights polysomnogram is 15min or<br>less (5) The presence of at least one: MSLT shows mean sleep<br>latency of 8 min or less OR total 24hr sleep time of 660 min or<br>longer (typically 12-14 hrs) on 24-hr polysonography monitoring<br>(performed after the correction of chronic sleep deprivation) or by<br>wrist actigraphy in assoc with a sleep log (avg over at least 7 days<br>with unrestricted sleep)  AND (6) hypersomolence or MSLT findings<br>are not better explained by another sleep disorder, medical or<br>neurologic disorder, mental disorder, med use or substance abuse.|
||For continuation, use has resulted in a reduction in frequency of<br>cataplexy attacks compared to baseline OR use has resulted in a<br>reduction in excessive daytime sleepiness (EDS) as measured by<br>improvement in Epworth Sleepiness Scale (ESS) measurements or<br>Maintenance of Wakefulness Test (MWT) compared to baseline.|

## **Zyvox** 

## **Products Affected** 

- _linezolid oral suspension reconstituted_ 

- _linezolid oral tablet_ 

|**PA Criteria**|**Criteria Details**|
|---|---|
|**Exclusion**<br>**Criteria**||
|**Required**<br>**Medical**<br>**Information**|vancomycin-resistant enterococcus faecium (VRE) infection OR<br>methicillin-resistant S. aureus (MRSA) infection. Or Infection that is<br>caused by other susceptible gram-positive organisms.|
|**Age**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Prescriber**<br>**Restrictions**||
|**Coverage**<br>**Duration**|30 days. 1 year for MDR-TB, XDR-TB, non-tuberculous<br>mycobacterial infection.|
|**Other Criteria**|If individual started treatment with Linezolid in the hospital and<br>requires continued outpatient therapy for an organism susceptible<br>to linezolid. For diagnosis of pulmonary multidrug-resistant<br>tuberculosis (MDR-TB) or pulmonary extensively drug-resistant<br>tuberculosis (XDR-TB) (WHO 2019), linezolid will be used in<br>combination with other anti-infectives (WHO 2019). For non-<br>tuberculous mycobacterial infection (including but not limited to M.<br>fortuitum) (ATS/ERS/ESCMID/IDSA 2020) AND will be used in<br>combination with other anti-infectives (ATS/ERS/ESCMID/IDSA<br>2020).|
|**Indications**|All Medically-accepted Indications.|
|**Off Label Uses**||
|**Part B**<br>**Prerequisite**|No|
